<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p34 ft3">AGREEMENT BETWEEN THE GOVERNMENT OF THE KING- DOM OF SWEDEN AND THE GOVERNMENT OF THE RE- PUBLIC OF SEYCHELLES FOR THE EXCHANGE OF INFOR- MATION RELATING TO TAX MATTERS</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p35 ft18"><SPAN class="ft17">Bilaga </SPAN>Prop. 2012/13:87 (√ñvers√§ttning)</P>
<P class="p36 ft3">AVTAL MELLAN KONUNGA-</P>
<P class="p37 ft3">RIKET SVERIGES REGERING</P>
<P class="p37 ft3">OCH REPUBLIKEN SEYCHEL-</P>
<P class="p15 ft3">LERNAS REGERING OM UT-</P>
<P class="p15 ft3">BYTE AV UPPLYSNINGAR I</P>
<P class="p38 ft3">SKATTE√ÑRENDEN</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p39 ft3">The Government of the Kingdom of Sweden and the Government of the Republic of Seychelles, desiring to conclude an Agreement for the exchange of information relating to tax matters, have agreed as follows:</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p39 ft5">Konungariket Sveriges regering och Republiken Seychellernas regering, som √∂nskar ing√• ett avtal om utbyte av upplysningar i skatte√§renden, har kommit √∂verens om f√∂ljande:</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p15 ft19">Article 1</P>
<P class="p40 ft4">Object and scope of the Agreement</P>
<P class="p41 ft3">1. The competent authorities of the Contracting Parties shall provide assistance through exchange of information that is foreseeably relevant to the administration and enforcement of the domestic laws of the Contracting Parties concerning taxes covered by this Agreement. Such information shall include information that is foreseeably relevant to the determination, assessment and collection of such taxes, the recovery and enforcement of tax claims, or the investigation or prosecution of tax matters. Information shall be exchanged in accordance with the provisions of this Agreement and shall be treated as confidential in the manner provided in Article 8. The rights and safeguards secured to persons by the laws or administrative practice of the requested Party remain applicable to the extent that they do not unduly prevent or delay effective ex-</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<TABLE id="IlI1I1IlIIIl1IlI1ll11I11l" cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t4"></TABLE>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_6">


<DIV>
<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1_1">
<P class="p15 ft3">change of information.</P>
<P class="p46 ft5">2. This Agreement shall not affect the application in the Contracting Parties of the rules on mutual legal assistance in criminal matters.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_1_2">
<P class="p47 ft5">effektivt utbyte av upplysningar. 2. Detta avtal ska inte p√•verka</P>
<P class="p48 ft5">till√§mpningen i de avtalsslutande parterna av best√§mmelserna om √∂msesidig r√§ttslig hj√§lp i brottm√•l.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<TABLE id="lI1Il1l1l1I1l11lIl11I11Il" cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t5"></TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_3">
<DIV id="id_1_3_1">
<P class="p39 ft5">A requested Party is not obligated to provide information which is neither held by its authorities nor in the possession or control of persons who are within its territorial jurisdiction.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_3_2">
<P class="p39 ft5">Den anmodade parten √§r inte skyldig att l√§mna upplysningar som varken innehas av dess myndigheter eller innehas eller kontrolleras av personer inom dess jurisdiktion.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_4">
<TABLE id="IlllIIl1Il1l1I11IlI1ll1II" cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t6"></TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_5">
<DIV id="id_1_5_1">
<P class="p39 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft22">The taxes which are the subject of this Agreement are taxes of every kind and description imposed in the Contracting Parties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p39 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft23">This Agreement shall also apply to any identical or substantially similar taxes imposed after the date of signature of the Agreement in addition to or in place of the existing taxes. The competent authorities of the Contracting Parties shall notify each other of any substantial changes to the taxation and related information gathering measures covered by the Agreement.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_5_2">
<P class="p39 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">De skatter som omfattas av detta avtal √§r skatter av varje slag och beskaffenhet som tas ut i de avtalsslutande parterna.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p39 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">Detta avtal till√§mpas √§ven p√• skatter av samma eller i huvudsak likartat slag som efter undertecknandet av avtalet tas ut vid sidan av eller i st√§llet f√∂r de f√∂r n√§rvarande utg√•ende skatterna. De beh√∂riga myndigheterna i de avtalsslutande parterna ska meddela varandra om de v√§sentliga √§ndringar som gjorts r√∂rande den skattelagstiftning och de √•tg√§rder f√∂r att inh√§mta upplysningar som omfattas av avtalet.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_6">
<TABLE id="I11l11I1Il1Il1I1lIllIlI11" cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t7"></TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_7">
<DIV id="id_1_7_1">
<P class="p39 ft5">1. For the purposes of this Agreement, unless otherwise defined:</P>
<P class="p49 ft5">a) the term ‚ÄùSeychelles‚Äù means the territory of the Republic of Seychelles including its exclusive</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_7_2">
<P class="p39 ft3">1. Om inte annat anges, har vid till√§mpningen av detta avtal f√∂ljande uttryck nedan angiven betydelse:</P>
<P class="p50 ft5">a) ‚ÄùSeychellerna‚Äù avser Republiken Seychellernas territorium inklusive dess exklusiva ekonomiska</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p15 ft3">Prop. 2012/13:87</P>
<P class="p33 ft3">6</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_7">


<DIV>
<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p51 ft3">economic zone and continental shelf where Seychelles exercises sovereign rights and jurisdiction in conformity with the provisions of the United Nations Convention on the Law of the Sea;</P>
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">the term ‚ÄùSweden‚Äù means the Kingdom of Sweden and, when used in a geographical sense, includes the national territory, the territorial sea of Sweden as well as other maritime areas over which Sweden in accordance with international law exercises sovereign rights or jurisdiction;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p46 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft22">the term ‚ÄùContracting Party‚Äù means Sweden or Seychelles as the context requires;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p53 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">the term ‚Äùcompetent authority‚Äù means:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p54 ft3">(i) in Seychelles, the Minister of Finance or an authorised representative of the Minister of Finance; (ii) in Sweden, the Minister of Finance, his authorised representative or the authority which is designated as a competent authority for the purposes of this Agree-</P>
<P class="p48 ft3">ment;</P>
<P class="p55 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">the term ‚Äùperson‚Äù includes an individual, a company and any other body of persons;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p53 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft26">the term ‚Äùcompany‚Äù means any body corporate or any entity that is treated as a body corporate for tax purposes;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p55 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft27">the term ‚Äùpublicly traded company‚Äù means any company whose principal class of shares is listed on a recognised stock exchange provided its listed shares can be readily purchased or sold by the public. Shares can be purchased or sold ‚Äùby the public‚Äù if the purchase or sale of shares is not implicitly or explicitly restricted to a limited group of investors;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p56 ft5"><SPAN class="ft3">h)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft28">the term ‚Äùprincipal class of shares‚Äù means the class or classes of shares representing a majority</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">

<P class="p15 ft19">Article 5</P>
<P class="p80 ft17">Exchange of information upon request</P>
<P class="p81 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft26">The competent authority of the requested Party shall provide upon request information for the purposes referred to in Article 1. Such information shall be exchanged without regard to whether the conduct being investigated would constitute a crime under the laws of the requested Party if such conduct occurred in the requested Party.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p82 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">If the information in the possession of the competent authority of the requested Party is not sufficient to enable it to comply with the request for information, that Party shall use all relevant information gathering measures to provide the applicant Party with the information requested, notwithstanding that the requested Party may not need such information for its own tax purposes.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p82 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft26">If specifically requested by the competent authority of an applicant Party, the competent authority of the requested Party shall provide information under this Article, to the extent allowable under its domestic laws, in the form of depositions of witnesses and authenticated copies of original records.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p68 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft27">A Contracting Party may allow representatives of the competent authority of the other Contracting Party to enter the territory of the </SPAN><NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> Party to interview individuals and examine records with the written consent of the persons concerned. <P class="p106 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">If the request referred to in paragraph 2 is acceded to, the competent authority of the Contracting Party conducting the examination shall, as soon as possible, notify the competent authority of the other Party about the time and place of the examination, the authority or official designated to carry out the examination and the</SPAN></P>

<P class="p15 ft4">Possibility of declining a request</P>
<P class="p113 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The requested Party shall not be required to obtain or provide information that the applicant Party would not be able to obtain under its own laws for purposes of the administration or enforcement of its own tax laws. <P class="p114 ft20"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft42">The provisions of this Agreement shall not impose on a Contracting Party the obligation to supply information which would disclose any trade, business, industrial, commercial or professional secret or trade process. <P class="p115 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft24">The provisions of this Agreement shall not impose on a Contracting Party the obligation to obtain or provide information, which would reveal confidential communications between a client and an attorney, solicitor or other admitted legal representative where such communications are:</SPAN></P>
